			<span class="sbi-screenreader">🏓 Know Your Lines, Play Your Game 🎯

Before you se</span>
			<svg class="svg-inline--fa fa-clone fa-w-16 sbi_lightbox_carousel_icon" aria-hidden="true" aria-label="Clone" data-fa-proƒcessed="" data-prefix="far" data-icon="clone" role="img" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 512 512">
                    <path fill="currentColor" d="M464 0H144c-26.51 0-48 21.49-48 48v48H48c-26.51 0-48 21.49-48 48v320c0 26.51 21.49 48 48 48h320c26.51 0 48-21.49 48-48v-48h48c26.51 0 48-21.49 48-48V48c0-26.51-21.49-48-48-48zM362 464H54a6 6 0 0 1-6-6V150a6 6 0 0 1 6-6h42v224c0 26.51 21.49 48 48 48h224v42a6 6 0 0 1-6 6zm96-96H150a6 6 0 0 1-6-6V54a6 6 0 0 1 6-6h308a6 6 0 0 1 6 6v308a6 6 0 0 1-6 6z"></path>
                </svg>						<img width="1000" height="560" src="https://racketroyalty.com/wp-content/plugins/instagram-feed/img/placeholder.png" alt="🏓 Know Your Lines, Play Your Game 🎯

Before you serve it up, get familiar with the lines on a pickleball court!

✨ Centerline: Splits the court into left &amp; right service areas.
✨ Non-Volley Line: 7 feet from the net, marking the “kitchen” (no volleying here!).
✨ Service Lines: Where your serve begins.

The kitchen keeps rallies fair, stopping players from smashing the ball right at the net. Whether you’re on concrete, asphalt, hardwood, or even grass - the lines stay the same.

Pro tip: you can even set up a pickleball court on a tennis court! 🎾 

Knowing your court = leveling up your game.
Follow us for more pickleball tips!

✔️ Prevents chips + scratches
✔️ Keeps the face clean + grippy
✔️ Helps your paddle last longer

function uc_blog_card_slider_elementor_19033e7d_start(){
	
  var objWrapper = jQuery('#uc_blog_card_slider_elementor_19033e7d');


   var options = {
      effect: 'fade',
      loop: true,
      mousewheel: false,
            autoplay: {delay:5000},
            mousewheel: {
        invert: false,
      },
      pagination: {
        el: '.blog-slider__pagination',
        clickable: true,
      }
    };
  
	var swiper = new Swiper('#uc_blog_card_slider_elementor_19033e7d', options);
        
    objWrapper.on("uc_ajax_refreshed", function(){
		swiper.loopDestroy();
		swiper = new Swiper('#uc_blog_card_slider_elementor_19033e7d', options);
    });
        

  jQuery("#uc_blog_card_slider_elementor_19033e7d").hover(function() {
    (this).swiper.autoplay.stop();
}, function() {
    (this).swiper.autoplay.start();
});


}setTimeout(function(){if(jQuery("#uc_blog_card_slider_elementor_19033e7d").length) uc_blog_card_slider_elementor_19033e7d_start(); else
	jQuery( document ).on( 'elementor/popup/show', () => { if(jQuery("#uc_blog_card_slider_elementor_19033e7d").length) uc_blog_card_slider_elementor_19033e7d_start();});},100);
});

jQuery(document).ready(function(){
  
  function showArrow(pixels){
  
     jQuery(window).scroll(function () {
        if (jQuery(this).scrollTop() > pixels) {
           jQuery('#uc_ue_scroll_to_top_elementor_b4edadd').fadeIn(300);
        } else {
           jQuery('#uc_ue_scroll_to_top_elementor_b4edadd').fadeOut(300);
        }
     });
  
  }
  
    
    
    jQuery('#uc_ue_scroll_to_top_elementor_b4edadd .ue-scroll-to-cta').click(function () {
       		   jQuery('body,html').animate({
				scrollTop: 0
		   }, 300 );
                  });
 });
